gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (
            f"Module generation failed:\nstdout: {gen_result.stdout}\nstderr: {gen_result.stderr}"
        )

        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")

tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_linear_transform_javascri0')
run_scripts = {'cpp': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.cpp'), 'javascript': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_test...sixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.py'), 'rust': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.rs')}
gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (
            f"Module generation failed:\nstdout: {gen_result.stdout}\nstderr: {gen_result.stderr}"
        )
E       AssertionError: Module generation failed:
E         stdout: 
E         stderr: /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);

entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', 'dynamic_buffer.py']
run_scripts = {'cpp': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.cpp'), 'javascript': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_test...sixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.py'), 'rust': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.rs')}

entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', 'dynamic_buffer.py']
case_data = {'expected': [{'id': '10', 'name': 'EVE', 'value': '500'}, {'id': '12', 'name': 'GRACE', 'value': '700'}, {'id': '13',...name': 'grace', 'status': 'active', 'value': '700'}, {'id': '13', 'name': 'hank', 'status': 'active', 'value': '800'}]}
lang = 'python'
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_filter_and_transform_comb0')
run_scripts = {'cpp': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.cpp'), 'javascript': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_test...sixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.py'), 'rust': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.rs')}
gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (
            f"Module generation failed:\nstdout: {gen_result.stdout}\nstderr: {gen_result.stderr}"
        )
E       AssertionError: Module generation failed:
E         stdout: 
E         stderr: /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1053: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'

lang = 'javascript'
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_add_constant_column_javas0')
run_scripts = {'cpp': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.cpp'), 'javascript': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_test...sixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.py'), 'rust': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.rs')}
gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (
            f"Module generation failed:\nstdout: {gen_result.stdout}\nstderr: {gen_result.stderr}"
        )
E       AssertionError: Module generation failed:
E         stdout: 
E         stderr: /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1053: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_index.txt`);
E         Traceback (most recent call last):

E                     ^^^^
E         NameError: name 'Dict' is not defined. Did you mean: 'dict'?

gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (
            f"Module generation failed:\nstdout: {gen_result.stdout}\nstderr: {gen_result.stderr}"
        )
E       AssertionError: Module generation failed:
E         stdout: 
E         stderr: /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1053: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_index.txt`);
E         Traceback (most recent call last):
E           File "/workspace/dynamic_buffer.py", line 46, in <module>
E             class PrefixTransform:
E           File "/workspace/dynamic_buffer.py", line 51, in PrefixTransform
E             params: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
E                     ^^^^
E         NameError: name 'Dict' is not defined. Did you mean: 'dict'?
E         
E       assert 1 == 0
E        +  where 1 = CompletedProcess(args=['uv', 'run', 'dynamic_buffer.py', 'dynamic_py_buffer', '--output', '/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_copy_column_python_0', '--sample', '/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_copy_column_python_0/sample', '--python'], returncode=1, stdout='', stderr='/workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence \'\\{\'\n  if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\\{{key}}_row_\\{{index}}.json`);\n/workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence \'\\{\'\n  if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\\{{key}}_row_\\{{index}}.json`);\n/workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1053: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence \'\\{\'\n  return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\\{{key}}_index.txt`);\nTraceback (most recent call last):\n  File "/workspace/dynamic_buffer.py", line 46, in <module>\n    class PrefixTransform:\n  File "/workspace/dynamic_buffer.py", line 51, in PrefixTransform\n    params: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)\n            ^^^^\nNameError: name \'Dict\' is not defined. run_scripts = {'cpp': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.cpp'), 'javascript': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_test...sixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.py'), 'rust': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.rs')}
gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (
            f"Module generation failed:\nstdout: {gen_result.stdout}\nstderr: {gen_result.stderr}"
        )
E       AssertionError: Module generation failed:
E         stdout: 
E         stderr: /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1053: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_index.txt`);
E         Traceback (most recent call last):
E           File "/workspace/dynamic_buffer.py", line 46, in <module>

E                     ^^^^
E         NameError: name 'Dict' is not defined. Did you mean: 'dict'?

gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (
            f"Module generation failed:\nstdout: {gen_result.stdout}\nstderr: {gen_result.stderr}"
        )
E       AssertionError: Module generation failed:
E         stdout: 
E         stderr: /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
E         /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1053: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_index.txt`);

            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[

gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (
            f"Module generation failed:\nstdout: {gen_result.stdout}\nstderr: {gen_result.stderr}"
        )
E       AssertionError: Module generation failed:

E         stderr: /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'

            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"

                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",

                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]

                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )

            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")

gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (
            f"Module generation failed:\nstdout: {gen_result.stdout}\nstderr: {gen_result.stderr}"
        )
E       AssertionError: Module generation failed:

gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")

        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],

        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,

        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")

case_data = {'expected': [{'amount': '50', 'id': '101', 'running_total': '50'}, {'amount': '75', 'id': '102', 'running_total': '12...id': '104'}, {'active': 'false', 'amount': '200', 'id': '105'}, {'active': 'true', 'amount': '100', 'id': '106'}, ...]}
lang = 'javascript'
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_combined_filter_cumsum_ja0')
run_scripts = {'cpp': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.cpp'), 'javascript': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_test...sixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.py'), 'rust': PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/run.rs')}
gen_timeout = 10, compile_timeout = 60, run_timeout = 30

    def run_transform_test(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        case_data: dict[str, Any],
        lang: str,
        tmp_path: Path,
        run_scripts: dict[str, Path],
        gen_timeout: int = 10,
        compile_timeout: int = 60,
        run_timeout: int = 30,
    ) -> None:
        """Run a transform test case.
    
        Args:
            entrypoint_argv: The entrypoint command as argv list
            case_data: Dict with input, output, test_data, expected keys
            lang: Language to test ("python", "javascript", "cpp", or "rust")
            tmp_path: Temporary directory for test files (sample, data, output)
            run_scripts: Dict mapping language to run script path
            gen_timeout: Timeout in seconds for module generation
            compile_timeout: Timeout in seconds for compilation (C++/Rust)
            run_timeout: Timeout in seconds for execution
        """
        # 1. Setup sample directory in tmp_path
        sample_dir = tmp_path / "sample"
        sample_dir.mkdir()
        write_csv(sample_dir / "input.csv", case_data["input"])
        write_csv(sample_dir / "output.csv", case_data["output"])
    
        # 2. Write test data
        write_csv(tmp_path / "data.csv", case_data["test_data"])
    
        # 3. Copy run script and set up commands
        # Note: Generation runs from workspace with absolute paths for sample/output
        # Execution runs from tmp_path where the generated module is
        workspace = Path.cwd()
    
        if lang == "python":
            module_name = "dynamic_py_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["python"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.py")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--python",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["uv", "run", "run.py", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "javascript":
            module_name = "dynamic_js_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["javascript"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.js")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--javascript",
            ]
            compile_cmds = []
            run_cmd = ["node", "run.js", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "cpp":
            module_name = "dynamic_cpp_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["cpp"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.cpp")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--cpp",
            ]
            # Compile: g++ -std=c++17 -I./dynamic_cpp_buffer -o run run.cpp ./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp
            compile_cmds = [[
                "g++", "-std=c++17",
                "-I./dynamic_cpp_buffer",
                "-o", "run",
                "run.cpp",
                "./dynamic_cpp_buffer/dynamic_preprocessor.cpp",
            ]]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        elif lang == "rust":
            module_name = "dynamic_rs_buffer"
            run_script = run_scripts["rust"]
            shutil.copy(run_script, tmp_path / "run.rs")
            gen_cmd = entrypoint_argv + [
                module_name,
                "--output",
                str(tmp_path),
                "--sample",
                str(sample_dir),
                "--rust",
            ]
            # Compile: cargo build --release in the module dir, then rustc
            compile_cmds = [
                ["cargo", "build", "--release"],  # Run in dynamic_rs_buffer subdir
                [
                    "rustc", "--edition", "2021",
                    "--extern", "dynamic_rs_buffer=dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/libdynamic_rs_buffer.rlib",
                    "-L", "dynamic_rs_buffer/target/release/deps",
                    "-o", "run",
                    "run.rs",
                ],
            ]
            run_cmd = ["./run", "data.csv"]
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported language: {lang}")
    
        # 4. Generate module (run from workspace where submission code lives)
        try:
            gen_result = subprocess.run(
                gen_cmd,
                cwd=workspace,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=gen_timeout,
            )
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            pytest.fail(f"TIMEOUT (generation): exceeded {gen_timeout}s - {' '.join(gen_cmd)}")
>       assert gen_result.returncode == 0, (
            f"Module generation failed:\nstdout: {gen_result.stdout}\nstderr: {gen_result.stderr}"
        )
E       AssertionError: Module generation failed:
E         stdout: 
E         stderr: /workspace/dynamic_buffer.py:1052: SyntaxWarning: invalid escape sequence '\{'
E           if (index >= 0) return path.join(this.cacheDir, `$\{{key}}_row_\{{index}}.json`);
